(Havas dispatch, 30th)

Warsaw: General Ryz-Smigly, Inspector General of the Army, set out for France yesterday with his entourage. He passed through Vienna today without stopping and continued westward at 2:30 pm. According to reports, Ryz-Smigly's mission is military in nature and limited to the mutual relations between France and Poland, which is exactly the same as the purpose of French Army Chief of Staff General Gamelin's visit to Warsaw some time ago. It is not true that Ryz-Smigly's trip to France was temporarily brought forward, as it was decided long ago that he would arrive in Paris before the French Army's autumn exercises. As for the claim that Ryz-Smigly's trip will bring about a major change in Polish foreign policy, it cannot be easily believed, because Polish policy is originally immutable. Any initiative taken internationally is based on the Franco-Polish alliance treaty of 1921 and there is no need for a change of course. The Warsaw "Daily Express" also recently stated that the Franco-Polish alliance treaty is of a permanent nature and has not changed in the slightest from the past. (Havas News Agency dispatch, 29th)

Establishment of the New Romanian Cabinet: Announcement of Policy Guidelines; Foreign Policy Remains Consistent; Strict Suppression of Political Agitation Internally 54

Bucharest, Romania – Following the resignation of the Tatarescu cabinet, the King reappointed Mr. Tatarescu to form a new cabinet, which has now been established. The allocation of key cabinet positions is as follows:

Prime Minister: Tatarescu; Deputy Prime Minister: Gugulescu (former Minister of Interior); Foreign Minister: Antonescu (former Finance Minister); Minister of Interior: Iuca; Finance Minister: Cancicov; Minister of Justice: Jianu.

Most of the new cabinet members belong to the Liberal Party, and many are reappointments from the previous cabinet. This marks Tatarescu's third cabinet. (Havas News Agency, 29th)

Bucharest, Romania – The new Tatarescu cabinet was formed last night. This morning at 1:00 AM, all cabinet members entered the palace to meet with King Carol and took the oath of office in the palace. Afterwards, Prime Minister Tatarescu addressed the press, outlining the new cabinet's policy guidelines. He stated that the new cabinet's policies would continue the established practices of the previous cabinet, with the aim of maintaining peace both domestically and internationally. The immediate priority is to ensure domestic stability, so that the public can share the benefits of prosperity. "All political groups, within the scope of existing laws, will still have the freedom to develop. All actions that overstep the boundaries and cause disruption will be suppressed before they occur and severely punished if they do occur. All semi-military organizations of various types nationwide, regardless of whether they belong to the right or left wing, will be disarmed." The government will also prohibit students from interfering in politics in order to rectify academic atmosphere. As for foreign policy, the government will continue to follow the established policies of the previous cabinet, which means creating a foundation for comprehensive and indivisible peace through a collective security system. Finally, Prime Minister Tatarescu addressed the issue of national defense, stating that the new cabinet would continue to increase the size of the army and would decide at the first cabinet meeting to submit a bill to Parliament requesting an additional allocation of 5,000,000,000 lei (Romanian currency) for the purchase of military equipment. (Havas News Agency, 30th)

Disagreement with the Prime Minister's Political Views: The Reason for the Former Foreign Minister's Resignation

What surprises political figures here the most is the absence of former Foreign Minister Titulescu from the new cabinet list. Since 1922, Titulescu has held key positions as Foreign Minister for fifteen years without interruption. The foreign policy pursued by Romania was formulated by him, and he implicitly held sway over the political arena in domestic affairs as well. This cabinet reshuffle, with Mr. Titulescu unexpectedly missing out, was truly beyond initial expectations. Political figures are discussing this matter, with differing opinions. Some say that during the Montreal Conference in June of this year, Titulescu, representing his country, attended the meeting. During the negotiations, he suddenly heard that nationalist factions in the country were very active, so he rushed back to his country from Montreal to strongly advocate to Prime Minister Tatarescu the harm of nationalist factions, threatening to resign. Although it did not cause a political crisis at the time, Tatarescu could not help but feel uneasy, thinking that Titulescu's move was detrimental to the authority of the government. This may be one of the reasons for Titulescu's dismissal. Tatarescu, after obtaining the consent of Liberal Party leader Bratianu, sent a telegram to Titulescu, expressing gratitude for his contributions to the country over the past fifteen years and his previous enthusiasm for cooperation, but stating that, due to circumstances, he had to form a unanimous government in order to faithfully implement the Liberal Party's policies. Titulescu himself is currently vacationing in Eaux, France. After hearing the news of the cabinet reshuffle, he immediately stated that he would not criticize this move for the time being and that he would reserve his right to take any political action in the future. (Havas News Agency, 29th)

Holding a Gun in One Hand and a Hoe in the Other: Japan's Immigration Plan for the Northeast; 1 Million Households, 5 Million People to Be Moved in the Next 20 Years; Cultivating Fertile Land Drives the Northeast's Farmers to the Brink of Ruin 59

Special Dispatch from the China United News Agency – To solve the domestic difficulties of "overpopulation and insufficient land," Japanese imperialism has, since the September 18th Incident, intensified its exploitation of the people of the Northeast through political and economic means, and has actively implemented a policy of collective agricultural immigration, hoping to adjust the rural population issue and realize a rural regeneration plan. However, under the fierce impact of this policy, the farmers of Northeast China can only rely on the barren land left over after exploitation to live in hunger and cold. According to investigations, the total number of Japanese residents in Manchuria since the September 18th Incident has been less than one million, and most of them are related to employees of the South Manchuria Railway Company and the Kwantung Leased Territory. There are actually no genuine agricultural immigrants. After the September 18th Incident, the puppet government, following the wishes of the Japanese, made all facilities suitable for the needs of the Japanese, and at the same time, due to the increase in the military strength of the Kwantung Army and the number of Japanese officials, the number of Japanese people suddenly increased by 70,000 in less than two months, and their residential area has spread to various inland rural villages in Manchuria. At the same time, the Japanese Ministry of Colonial Affairs took advantage of various preferential conditions obtained through armed aggression and began implementing a collective agricultural immigration policy in October of the 21st year. The Japanese who were relocated into the customs at that time were all demobilized soldiers from various counties in the domestic Northeast who were experienced in farming and animal husbandry, totaling 500 people. The relocation site was Jiamusi, downstream of the Songhua River. In February of the 22nd year, they were sent to Yongping Town, where they were divided into twelve tribes, each operating farming and animal husbandry. The Japanese Ministry of Colonial Affairs and the Kwantung Army authorities, in order to strengthen their production capacity, also declared the town to implement an autonomous village system, and recruited families to immigrate together, so that they could permanently settle in the area. The area they are now cultivating totals 160 Japanese mu for soybeans, 120 Japanese mu for wheat, 80 Japanese mu for millet, and 60 Japanese mu for rice. In terms of animal husbandry, there are more than 700 heads of horses, cattle, pigs, sheep, etc. Other side businesses, such as manufacturing wheat flour, soybean oil, and soy sauce, are also quite developed. In July of the 22nd year, the second immigration was implemented, also with 500 people, relocated to Qihuli (Hunan Camp) adjacent to Yongfeng Town. This group of immigrants mainly engaged in agriculture, cultivating soybeans on 170 Japanese mu, wheat on 150 Japanese mu, and sorghum on 55 Japanese mu, in addition to 31 Japanese mu of paddy fields, with excellent harvests. The third immigration site was in Suiling (Wangrongmiao), also with 500 people, cultivating an area of 14,000 Japanese mu, mainly planting wheat and soybeans. In terms of animal husbandry, sheep production was also quite prosperous. The above three were all so-called trial immigrations, and because they were under the assistance of armed forces, the results gave the Japanese authorities satisfactory answers. Therefore, the Ministry of Colonial Affairs again gathered more than 400 people last summer, gave them strict training, and crossed the border in September to engage in pioneering activities in various counties of Heilongjiang. This is the situation of the fourth immigration. Recently, the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, the Army Ministry, and the Kwantung Army authorities, in view of the excellent results of several past immigrations, have decided to allocate more than 600 million yen to implement a large-scale 20-year immigration plan to Manchuria (from 1937 to 1957), relocating 1 million households, totaling 5 million people, and have set the coming year to begin moving in 10,000 households, totaling 50,000 people. The relocation sites are as follows: (1) Northern Manchuria: 500,000 households (2.5 million people); (2) Suburbs of Shenyang, Harbin, Changchun, Jinzhou: Undetermined number of immigrants; Rehe and Inner Mongolia areas: Undetermined number of pastoral immigrants; (3) Forest areas of Jilin Province: Undetermined number of forestry immigrants; Gold mining immigrants near Mohe in Heilongjiang: Undetermined number of immigrants. Under such severe destruction, most of the farmers in the Northeast have already armed themselves and organized or participated in volunteer armies to defend their own farmland. They attacked Qihuli, the reclaimed land of the second collective agricultural immigration by Japan, last spring, causing them heavy losses. After learning this lesson, they have deeply recognized the strength of the volunteer army's fighting power, so in addition to hoes, each person carries a rifle to guard against attacks by the volunteer army, and also performs the task of reconnaissance for the Kwantung Army.

Guangxi Army Invades Southern Guangdong Province, Traffic Below Liangyang is Cut Off, Government Agencies Relocated, Guangxi Army Occupies Qinzhou in One Route and Enters Gao-Lei in Another 83

Guangzhou correspondence: Although the Central Government has sent senior officials to Guangxi to mediate the Guangxi affair, the mediation over the past half month has ultimately been ineffective due to Li and Bai's strong attitude. At present, the Guangxi army has taken action to break through and invade Guangdong. Since Qinzhou, Lianzhou, Gaozhou, and Leizhou, which border Guangxi and Guangdong, are located near the sea and adjacent to the French Guangzhou Bay, in order to open up sea routes for transportation, it is inevitable to invade the southern part of Guangdong Province as a base for the Guangxi situation. Therefore, the important agencies in Nanning had already been relocated to Wuming in advance, using the natural barriers of mountains and rivers as a base. At the same time, plainclothes troops were sent to invade the four prefectures of Qinzhou, Lianzhou, Gaozhou, and Leizhou in Guangdong. These plainclothes troops of the Guangxi army had already dispersed into the Guangdong border before the 21st of this month. Therefore, on the 22nd, the agencies in Lianzhou and Beihai were disturbed once by the invading vanguard of the Guangxi army. The Hepu County Government and the Beihai branch of the Provincial Bank have packed up and moved important documents and silver coins, as well as tax revenue. All telephone bureaus and radio bureaus have also moved their equipment. Municipal bureaus, public security bureaus, and other agencies have also prepared to leave the city with their files. Later, it was discovered that the vanguard of the Guangxi army had taken the road through Yulin, Bobai, Shahezai, and arrived at Shisun on the evening of the 21st. (Shisun is about 130 li from Lianzhou in Guangdong). At the same time, a part of the Guangxi army entered the Guangdong territory of Luwu through Nanxiang. As a result, the Qinzhou government office moved after hearing the news. On the 24th of this month, the official troops of the Guangxi army arrived one after another. It is said that the Guangxi army's Su Zuxin division, about 4,000 to 5,000 people, entered Guangdong's Gaozhou and Leizhou from Yulin and Bobai. The Guangxi army's Zhou Zuhuang division, about 7,000 to 8,000 people, entered the Liangyang area (Yangjiang and Yangchun counties) was the Weng Zhaoyuan division. Therefore, since the 25th, Guangxi troops have been found everywhere in Liangyang, Gaozhou, Leizhou, Qinzhou, and Kangzhou in Guangdong Province. All highways south of Liangyang have been closed, and telecommunications traffic has also been cut off. Most of the tax revenue in the southern part has been intercepted by the Guangxi army. After the 26th, long-distance buses on the main highways from Kaiping County's Changsha to Meicha, and from Hua County to Leizhou and Suixi, were requisitioned by the Guangxi army for transporting troops. The Guangxi army's Zhou Zuhuang and Weng Zhaoyuan units occupied Lianjiang City on the 25th, passed through Anpu on the 26th, and arrived at Suixi on the 27th. Government officials fled to Guangzhou Bay. On the 28th, officials from Huaxian and Xinyi also fled to Meichashi (under Gaozhou). The Southern District Pacification Commissioner's Office has sent an urgent telegram requesting assistance. (August 29th)

Guangdong Province Counties Suffer Hurricane Disaster, Haifeng and Lufeng Salt Fields Washed Away by Tides, More Than Half of the Shops in Nanshui, Zhongshan Collapse, More Than a Thousand People Drowned in Haiyan District, Taishan 84

Guangzhou Correspondence: In mid-August, various counties in Guangdong Province were hit by hurricanes. All coastal areas, such as Haifeng, Lufeng, Huiyang, and Boluo in the eastern district, Zhaoqing and Taishan in the western district, Maoming Shuidong in the southern district, and Zhongshan in the central district, have suffered huge losses, especially in Haifeng, Zhongshan, and Taishan counties. According to investigations, Haifeng and Lufeng were hit by a hurricane and tidal wave on the 18th of the month. In the Jieshi area of Lufeng, more than 20 salt fields collapsed, and dozens of ships sank. In Yuanfeng Township in the first district of Haifeng, and Dawai She in the third district, the paddy fields and houses were flooded by the tidal wave caused by the hurricane. The water in the inner streets was more than three feet high. The fourth district became a swamp, and most of the roads were destroyed. The seawater flooded to the foot of Nanshan Mountain, and the breached levee caused the salt fields to be submerged. More than 30 thatched houses in Zhelang Township were blown down, and more than 20 fishing boats went missing. Zhongshan County is also a coastal area. Fortunately, there is a huge harbor to buffer the force of the wind; otherwise, the losses from this typhoon would have been unimaginable. However, during this typhoon, civilian houses collapsed in Shiqi, and seawater flooded the streets to a depth of two feet. In Qianshan, the water was knee-deep. Telephone and street light poles and wires in the second, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts of the county were completely broken. The water in the sand fields was more than ten feet high, and dozens of houses collapsed in the second district. The disaster in the seventh district was unprecedented. The typhoon started in this area at about 3:00 a.m. on the 16th. Nanshui port was at the forefront because of its proximity to the sea. More than 50 houses were blown down in the entire port, and refugees were trapped on isolated islands, cut off from food and drinking water. Of the more than 200 fishing boats in the nearby fishing villages, only about 30 remained after the windstorm, which was also very tragic. The next day, people from all walks of life in the county sent people to provide relief with dry food and fresh water, and those who had no home to return to were transported back to the county seat for resettlement. In Taishan County, the Haiyan district of the county suffered the worst damage from the typhoon on the evening of the 16th. Xiaoluo Township in this district is located near the sea and has a high embankment to protect it from the tides. The embankment was built in the Shengqing Qianlong era. Various surnames lived together in the embankment, with a population of about 5,000, mostly making a living by fishing and farming. All was peaceful. Unexpectedly, on the night of August 16, a hurricane struck, and the embankment collapsed, and seawater rushed in. Eight out of ten houses in the entire village collapsed, and more than a thousand people drowned. Livestock, food, and utensils were all washed away. More than 4,000 refugees cried on the embankment, homeless, starving and waiting for help. It was a disaster unprecedented in the village for more than 200 years. In addition, all the embankments in the Haiyan district were breached by the water. In recent days, more than 470 corpses have been found, more than 1,700 houses have collapsed, and more than 1,000 refugees have been displaced. Recently, the county party headquarters has telegraphed the provincial authorities about the disaster and requested the government to allocate funds for emergency relief as soon as possible. (August 29th)

Internal Strife Among Remnant Bandits in Western Fujian, Bandit Leader Qiu Jinsheng Removed from Office, Many Bandits Surrender Themselves to the District Office 85

Xiamen Correspondence: The remnant bandits in western Fujian have the pseudo "Southwestern Fujian Military and Political Committee" as their highest authority, commanding the bandit forces in Yan, Yong, Ping, Lian, and Shang in western Fujian, as well as Jing, He, Pu, Yun, and Zhao counties in Zhangzhou in southern Fujian. Zhang Dingcheng serves as chairman, Deng Zihui as vice chairman, and Tan Zhenlin and others as members. Recently, due to conflicts of interest, internal strife has occurred. Qiu Jinsheng, the pseudo eighth regiment leader, commander of the third anti-Japanese war zone, and member of the Southwestern Fujian Military and Political Committee, was removed from his concurrent positions as commander of the third district and member of the military and political committee by the pseudo Southwestern Fujian Military and Political Committee. At the same time, Chen Chaopan, the pseudo deputy chairman of the Yan South Zhang County Committee, was removed from all concurrent positions and expelled from the party for four months. The militia team in Yanxiang, Longyan County, recently searched bandit documents and found the newly published "Red Flag, Issue 4," which contained the process of Qiu's removal and the "Southwestern Fujian Military and Political Committee's" announcement of Qiu's crimes. It is said that Qiu is from Longyan and is the most powerful of the bandits. He gained the status of bandit leader in Yan and Yong. His eighth regiment is the main force of the bandits in western Fujian. He is usually arrogant and indulgent, and has conflicts with the chief of staff sent to the area by the pseudo Military and Political Committee. They are incompatible with each other, and he is also incompatible with the political commissar of the area. Many of the orders issued by the pseudo Southwestern Fujian Military and Political Committee are disobeyed, which has long been displeasing to Zhang Dingcheng. Therefore, this removal occurred. Although Qiu was forced to relinquish his concurrent positions as commander of the third district and member of the military and political committee, he still serves as the pseudo eighth regiment leader. After his removal, he was extremely indignant and tried to overthrow Zhang Dingcheng. Furthermore, there is also fierce infighting between Zhang Dingcheng and Deng Zihui. As for the reasons for Chen Chaopan's punishment, it is because he is at odds with Wei Jinshui, the chairman of the pseudo Yan South Zhang County Committee. This shows the intensity of the infighting among the bandits. The crimes of Qiu and Chen also show the depth of the corruption and deterioration of the bandits. Since the internal strife among the bandits, in the past week, many villagers in the fourth and sixth districts of Longyan who were forced to join the bandits have surrendered to the district office and the joint guarantee director with their guns. In Zhangzhou, since the 75th Division's Shi brigade suppressed the four counties of Jing, He, Ling, and Yi and recovered the Liangshan bandit den, after the news that bandit leader Zhang Changshui was shot and killed, the bandits along the Zhangzhou-Yian line on the Longyi Road have been eliminated. In the past week, the banditry in various counties in Zhangzhou has been relatively restrained. However, there are still bandit disturbances in Longyan and Zhangping in western Fujian. (August 27th)

After Yang Yongtai Takes Office in Hubei: Political Measures in Hubei Province; Comprehensive Renovation of Administrative Organs at Provincial, District, and County Levels; Implementing "Six Transformations" to Save Rural Areas with a "Four-in-One" System; Completion of Highway Network Construction; Wuhan as a Garden City 86

Hankou Correspondence: After enduring natural disasters and banditry, Hubei Province's key policies were progressing slowly. Only after Zhang Qun took office as Provincial Chairman were concrete plans made, but due to being summoned to the central government, he was unable to fully implement them. The central government, recognizing Hubei's crucial position, urgently sought to promote construction and specially appointed Yang Yongtai, Secretary-General of the Military Affairs Commission Chairman's Office, concurrently as head of Hubei's administration. He assumed office on New Year's Day this year and has now served for eight months. Under Yang's management and planning, coupled with abundant agricultural harvests and financial stability, significant progress has been made in political measures. At the beginning of his tenure, Yang published his political views, outlining several key points, and has since been systematically advancing these goals. The most prominent is the improvement of administrative organs. All departments and offices have implemented joint office operations to unify government orders. All civil servants are managed according to military discipline, sweeping away the past habits of procrastination and inefficiency. The atmosphere has been completely transformed. After self-rectification, all administrative affairs have become well-organized. Regarding civil affairs, administrative inspector districts have been reorganized, with the original eleven districts reduced to eight. County government organizations have been improved, with revised personnel quotas and salaries, saving expenses. The implementation of district offices is being carried out in phases, with the first phase covering twenty-four counties including Wuchang, and the second phase covering twenty-four counties including Jiayu. The original one hundred and twenty-eight districts have been reduced to eighty-eight. Training of Baojia (neighborhood watch) and consolidation of public security are all based on the district offices as the backbone. The public security bureaus located in the district office residences are merged into the county government to complete the connection of security and seek coordination of police administration. In the Jianghan River basin area, river police have been added, and river Baojia are being compiled and investigated. In terms of opium suppression, 6,678 opium dens have been closed, and 124 drug rehabilitation hospitals and centers have been established. 20,062 opium addicts have been forcibly rehabilitated, and 41,900 opium addicts have been rehabilitated voluntarily. 120,000 kilograms of drugs have been burned, and 340,000 opium addicts have been registered. Opium seedlings have been eradicated throughout the province. Regarding financial affairs, independent county finances have been implemented, with the establishment of collection offices and county treasuries. The revenue and expenditure auditing system adopts a detached system, so that accounting and financial accounting are separate and independent, helping each other. Rent collectors have been abolished and replaced with tax collection supervisors to avoid extortion. Business tax bureaus have also been reorganized across the board. Business tax revenue has exceeded the quota. After the deed tax was reorganized, revenue increased by one times compared to the previous year. Regarding land tax and land administration, the two are inherently one. Except for the land survey reports, which have only been completed in six counties, and future assistance from the central government for aerial surveying is still needed, the reorganization of land tax has been effectively implemented. The methods are: unified collection, renovated institutions, strict performance assessment, rigorous auditing, and equalization of tax rates, revised tax amounts, stipulating that each mu of high-grade land will be taxed at 1.2 dimes, medium-grade land at 1 dime, and low-grade land at 8 cents. Overly heavy taxes will be based on the original amount, and the payment of coupon taxes will be waived. Land tax has increased by 1.13 million annually, which, together with the original tax amount of 3.34 million, totals 4.47 million, exceeding the highest tax amount of 4.16 million in the fifth year of the Republic of China. It has also been decided that this year will be the land tax year. Using the Baojia system, households will be asked about land, and land will be asked about grain. In the future, income can be doubled due to the land survey. As for the tax arrears of various counties, totaling 6 million yuan, they are also being thoroughly cleared. Regarding rural relief, Yang has proposed the slogan of "scientific, industrialized, organized, cooperative, militarized, and disciplined agriculture," also known as the "Six Transformations" policy. It is also the so-called "four-in-one system of management, education, raising, and sanitation." In order to organize agricultural products and facilitate freight transportation, the Agricultural Products Consolidation and Marketing Office and the Agricultural Products Consolidation and Marketing Design Committee have been specially established, one as the executive agency and one as the design agency. Other measures such as the establishment of cooperative treasuries, simple agricultural warehouses, handling of agricultural product mortgages, encouraging land reclamation and animal husbandry, promoting tung tree planting, and improving cotton seeds, ramie, and silkworm industries are all being actively carried out. Moreover, the Jianghan River basin often suffers from floods, and other counties are prone to drought. A water conservancy design committee has been formed to conduct research. In the upper reaches of the Xiang River, the construction of flood control dams and reservoirs has already begun. Water conservancy loans are also being offered, with the scope of loans including (1) repairing dikes, (2) building sluices, (3) repairing culverts, (4) dredging ditches, (5) dredging river ports, and (6) other drainage and irrigation equipment. The annual interest rate is only set at four percent. In the midst of passive prevention, it is an active move to seek benefits. Farmers in various counties have all expressed their convenience. Regarding construction, in addition to repairing dikes for flood prevention and dredging ponds for drought prevention, the completion of the highway network is also important. Among them, the Bazhi section is the most difficult. This section runs from Badong through Jianshi to Enshi, with a length of 208.0 kilometers, all high mountains and steep ridges. It is now open to traffic. The Chongtong section from Chongyang to Tongshan, the Tongxin section from Tongshan to Xintanpu, the Xinyang section from Xintanpu to Yangxin, and the Xinji section from Xintanpu to the boundary marker on the Jiangxi border are all built and opened to traffic this year. Together with the previous ones, a total of 3,600 kilometers of highways have been built. In addition, sections such as Shilai, Chongping, Yangjie, Yangqi, Xituan, and Tuanliu are under construction and will soon be completed. Sections such as Shili, Shizhu, Xiantong, and Yiwu are still in the planning stage. As for the construction of the provincial capital, there has been even more amazing development. Yang's goal is to realize the idea of a garden city, so that people from other provinces are happy to invest, so that it will gradually become prosperous. With the opening of the Yuehan Railway, agricultural products may be concentrated in Wuchang. Therefore, the construction of Wuchang is superficially to prosper the city, but in reality, it is still to relieve the countryside. Regarding education, education funding has been restored to the budget, and accumulated arrears over the years have been cleared. This year's budget is one-third higher than last year's. It has been determined that popularizing literacy education is the criterion for implementing national crisis education. More than half of the counties have established popular literacy education committees. Lianbao (joint guarantee) primary schools are being promoted by district offices and are also showing results. Other measures such as summer military training for teachers and staff, teacher certification, and the implementation of a full-time system, as well as the opening of township personnel training institutes, have either been implemented or are still in preparation. Before the summer military training for teachers and staff, many did not want to participate, but in the end, they all complied. They have now been training for many days and will soon be able to complete the task.

Anhui North: Actively Building Highways; Most of the Main Lines Completed; County Roads Being Built in Sections 87

Bengbu Correspondence: The transportation infrastructure in northern Anhui was originally underdeveloped. In past years, county roads between various counties were mostly bumpy, undulating, rugged, and uneven. Traveling by car on them often felt like a roller coaster ride. In recent years, the Provincial Department of Construction has been actively carrying out the construction of highways, and the administrative authorities of various counties have also been repairing the original roads in stages, striving to improve them. Compared with the county roads of the past, there has been great progress. The main roads along the Jinpu Railway and the Changhuai area have been largely completed. Those that have not been completed are still being actively extended. According to information obtained from the Highway Bureau, the section of highway from Bengbu to Guzhen has recently been repaired under the supervision of the Bengu Road Engineering Office. Four-tenths of the entire section has been completed, and the rest is being worked on to ensure completion on schedule. The roadbed from Bengbu to Zhengyang has been surveyed by engineer Ding Gongnan of the Bengu Road Engineering Office under orders. The entire line is about to be completed. As soon as the survey is completed, construction will begin. The section of highway from Mingguang to Shuanggou (under the jurisdiction of Si) has been started after a joint survey by the governments of Xuyi and Si counties. The section from Linhuai to Jiangba is being actively prepared and surveyed by the Linjiang Highway Engineering Office. The budget for the intermediate culvert project has been approved by the Provincial Highway Bureau and submitted to the Department of Construction for review. The entire project will not be completed until next year. (28th)

Songjiang: Ta Yan Buddhist Temple Robbed 88

Ta Yan Buddhist Temple in Punan New Street was suddenly attacked by seven or eight robbers speaking a local dialect the day before yesterday (23rd). They knocked on the gate, tied up all the monks, and searched the temple for half an hour before escaping south. The abbot of the temple, Ren Zhao, checked the losses and found that more than twenty yuan in cash and clothing had been robbed. However, the abbot was afraid of making enemies with the bandits and did not dare to report it. Later, the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau learned of the incident and sent police to investigate. They have asked the General Bureau to investigate and arrest the bandits.

Verdict on Road Workers' Riot Case 90

In the case of the road workers of the Suxi Road in Zhouxin Town, Third District, who destroyed the Eighth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, 84 road workers were arrested at that time and sent to the court. After the preliminary investigation by Prosecutor Qian, 57 people, including Zhou Guangyi, were deemed to have insufficient evidence and were given a non-prosecution disposition. The rest, including Chen Hanchen, were prosecuted. After repeated summonses and investigations by Judge Liu, the verdict was announced yesterday. Chen Hanchen and others publicly gathered a crowd and used violence and coercion against public officials performing their duties in accordance with the law. Each was sentenced to six months of imprisonment. Yang Shoushan was found not guilty. Yang Bingchen, Wang Xiangkui, Wang Desheng, Zhang Longgen, Wu Kui, Wu Jichun, Li Guancheng, Xiong Delian, Yang Junkuan, Liu Deyu, Li Jinbiao, Wu Menghua, Ma Liangzhong, Wu Deshan, Wang Mingyuan, Jia Wenshan, Zhou Changlong, Yang Chuanfang, Wang Fengyou, and Zhou Lianfeng were all given a two-year suspended sentence. Chen Jie Arrives in Shanghai to Discuss Various Diplomatic Issues; Hopes for a Reasonable Resolution to the Chengdu Incident; No Concrete Plan for Economic Cooperation Has Been Proposed 106

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, Chen Jie, the Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, arrived in Shanghai at 11 PM the day before yesterday via the 5 PM express train. A Xin Sheng News Agency reporter met him on the train and conducted the following interview: (Question) After the Chengdu incident, what measures has the government taken, and what is the guiding principle? (Answer) This incident occurred on the 24th. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs received a telegram from Wu Zexiang, the special envoy stationed in Sichuan, on the following day, reporting the Chengdu riot and casualties among the people, including Japanese residents. At that time, Minister Zhang was still in Guling and preparing to return to Nanjing. He immediately reported the matter by telephone. Zhang flew back to Nanjing on the 26th, convened a special meeting, and consulted with key government officials to discuss investigation and response methods. On one hand, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs telegraphed the Sichuan Provincial Government to inquire about the details of the riot and the situation of Japanese residents, urging them to strictly suppress the situation, intensify the pursuit of the perpetrators, and earnestly protect foreign nationals. On the other hand, the Executive Yuan telegraphed Liu, the Chairman of Sichuan Province, ordering him to promptly investigate and punish local military and police personnel who failed to provide adequate protection, and to immediately dispatch personnel from the Ministry to Sichuan to investigate the truth. That evening, Suma, the secretary of the Japanese Embassy, visited Minister Zhang for other matters. Zhang immediately informed him of the situation he had heard and the government's handling of the matter, expressing deep regret and promising to do his best to seek a proper resolution based on a detailed report, with an open and sincere attitude, and fair and reasonable methods. He earnestly hoped that the Japanese side would also exercise patience and caution, and not allow a local incident to hinder the overall adjustment. The investigator's report on the case is expected to arrive in Nanjing shortly. The Japanese side has also dispatched Embassy Secretary Matsumura and Chongqing Consul Kasuya to investigate the matter, and it is expected that they will also provide a detailed report. This is the general process and guiding principle of the government's handling of this case. In short, the occurrence of this incident was truly unexpected by the government. The government has always paid great attention to the protection of foreign nationals. Based on the number of casualties among the Chengdu military and police and the situation described by Tanaka, who was rescued from the hospital by the Director of the Public Security Bureau, it can be seen that the situation at the time was critical and efforts were made to protect foreign nationals. Two principal offenders were executed by firing squad that same day. Today, the National Government reiterated the order to maintain friendly relations, which further demonstrates the government's clear attitude. (Question) Is there any concrete progress in Sino-Japanese economic cooperation? It is said that Wang Keyou will go north soon. Is this true? (Answer) Sino-Japanese economic cooperation in North China has been discussed for a long time, but no concrete plan has yet been proposed. Wang is expected by both sides to realize this matter, and it is hoped that he can go north as soon as possible to take charge of the process. (Question) When will the newly appointed ambassadors to Russia and the United States take office? (Answer) The newly appointed ambassador to Russia, Jiang, has returned to Nanjing from Guling and is currently preparing for the handover and arranging departure procedures. It is said that he will depart in October. Ambassador to the United States, Wang, must wait until September 3, after leading the World Games delegation back from Italy, before scheduling his departure to the United States. (Question) There have been many changes in overseas embassies and consulates recently. Have you heard of any guiding principles for these changes? (Answer) Since Minister Zhang took office, the Ministry has focused on adjusting diplomatic relations externally and adjusting staff internally. After performance appraisals, the adjustment of Ministry staff is largely complete. However, the scope of overseas missions is larger and there are more staff members. Many of them have served abroad for a long time and are unfamiliar with the domestic situation. At the same time, some internal staff are not very familiar with the overseas situation. It is being considered to transfer staff internally and externally, selecting outstanding personnel from overseas missions for internal use, and assigning internal staff who are qualified and capable of being trained to overseas positions. The intention of talent development is incorporated into the adjustment. It is said that Chen's visit to Shanghai this time is to take care of personal matters and there are no other tasks.

Wu Yue History and Geography Research Association Established Yesterday; Constitution Passed, President and Directors Appointed; Exhibition of Antiquities Divided into Three Categories: Pottery, etc. 109

The Wu Yue History and Geography Research Association, initiated by cultural leaders Cai Yuanpei, Yu Youren, Wu Zhihui, Ye Gongchuo, Wei Juxian, etc., held its inaugural meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. More than 60 people attended, including initiators Cai Yuanpei, Ye Gongchuo, Wei Juxian, and members from Nanjing, Hangzhou, Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Jiaxing, and other places, including Hu Puan, Ding Fubao, Xie Ruiling, Zheng Hongnian, Yang Kailing, Jian Youwen, Zhang Naiji, etc. Cai Yuanpei presided over the meeting, Wei Juxian recorded the minutes, and the constitution was passed on the spot, and officers were appointed. In order to arouse the members' interest in studying antiquities, the association also held an antiquities exhibition at the same time. People in Shanghai took advantage of the weekend holiday to visit the exhibition enthusiastically. The details are recorded as follows:

Exhibition of Antiquities

The antiquities displayed by the association yesterday were generally divided into three categories: pottery, stone tools, and porcelain. (1) Those belonging to pottery include pottery pots, pottery statues, pottery jars, pottery urns, pottery fragments, epitaphs, and bricks. (2) Those belonging to stone tools include stone shovels, stone axes, stone spears, stone arrowheads, and stone balls. (3) Those belonging to porcelain are arranged according to the era, divided into Han porcelain, Six Dynasties porcelain, Tang porcelain, Northern Song porcelain, and Southern Song porcelain. In addition, the paper model of the Warring States period bronze plate and the Song Guan kiln temporarily sent to the meeting by antique collectors are particularly unique. These antiquities were mostly discovered in Gudang in Zhejiang Province, Qianshanyang in Huzhou, and Quanshan, Yan City, and Yue City in Jiangsu Province. Some also came from Shanxi and Xiamen. Wei Juxian explained them separately and gave enthusiastic instructions. The audience was very interested.

Cai's Speech

Chairman Cai Yuanpei delivered an opening speech, saying, "Today is the inaugural meeting of the Wu Yue History and Geography Research Association. The purpose of our association is based on the successive discoveries of ancient stone tools and pottery in Gudang, Qianshanyang, Shaoxing, Jinshan, and other places, which provide sufficient historical reference value. It proves that the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang had a very high culture five or six thousand years ago, and it is certainly not as the legend says that Jiangsu and Zhejiang were still barbaric areas in the Spring and Autumn Period. Now, there must be many of these antiquities remaining in various parts of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. I hope that after the establishment of this association, members from various places can continue to discover more for research, so as to understand the evolution of history and the living conditions of our ancestors."

Adoption of Constitution

The constitution was then adopted as follows: (1) This association is named the Wu Yue History and Geography Research Association. (2) The purpose of this association is to study the history and geography of Wu Yue (temporarily limited to the land of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces). (3) Anyone who is interested in studying the history and geography of Wu Yue may apply for membership. After being introduced by a member, filling out a application form, and being approved by the board of directors, he/she will become a member of this association. (4) The expenses of this association shall be one yuan per year for membership fees. If it is not enough, with the approval of the council and the board of directors, donations may be raised. (5) This association shall have one president, two vice presidents, and a number of councilors, who shall be elected or appointed by each general meeting of members. They may be re-elected and re-appointed. This association shall have 11 executive directors, who shall be elected by the directors. (6) This association shall hold a general meeting of members once a year, which shall be convened by the president, and an executive board meeting once a month, which shall be convened by the secretary-general. (7) This association may publish various publications on Wu Yue culture, which shall be planned and handled by the Publication Committee. (8) This association shall be located in Shanghai, and may establish branches in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, and sub-branches in each county. (9) If there are any matters not covered in these bylaws, they may be amended by the General Assembly.

Appointment of Officers

(President) Cai Yuanpei, (Vice Presidents) Wu Zhihui, Niu Yongjian, (Councilors) Yu Youren, Kong Yongzhi, Zhang Puquan, Dai Jitao, Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Ye Yufu, Wang Shijie, Wang Yongbin, Weng Wenhao, Zhang Daofan, Wu Tiecheng, Zhou Fohai, Pan Gongzhan, Xu Shaodi, Xie Huisheng, Zhang Jingjiang, Chu Minyi, Liu Yazi, Li Genyuan, Hu Puan, Li Jizhi, Liu Yimou, Teng Gu, Ma Shuping, He Xufu, Wang Xiantang, Chen Xunci, Dong Yumo, Zou An, Zhu Kongyang, Ding Fubao, Chen Wanli, Zhang Naiji, Zheng Hongnian, Xuan Zhe, Jiang Hengyuan, Jian Youwen, Wu Kaisheng, Wang Yunwu, He Bingsong, Guan Baiyi, Hu Zhaochun, Zhang Feng, (Directors) Li Dachao, Jiang Jianbai, Dong Zuobin, Qiu Shanyuan, Liang Siyong, Hu Xiaoshi, Zhu Xizu, Zhou Xingcuo, Miao Fenglin, Gu Yangsheng, Jin Songcen, Hu Huaichen, Zhang Qichun, Chen Zhongfan, Sheng Xinfu, Hu Xingzhi, Zheng Shixu, Lu Simian, Jiang Shangwu, Zheng Zhenduo, Zhou Yutong, Zhang Shilu, Li Bingruo, Chen Gaoyong, Shen Junru, Wu Zelin, Liang Yuandong, Chen Zhuzun, Li Jianwu, Fu Shishuo, Wang Yong, Lu Kanru, Jiang Xuanyi, Teng Baiye, Shen Qinlu, Le Sibing, Cao Juren, Chen Rentao, Zhang Aying, Cheng Yuncen, Zong Libai, Zhang Shilin, Wu Zijing, Du Gangbai, Qian Huafu, He Zhenya, Hua Lin, Jin Guobao, Bao Ding, Mao Chang, Lin Huixiang, Hu Huisheng, Shen Weijun, Zhang Danfu, Ge Suicheng, Qiu Hanfang, Gu Xieguang, Zhu Hongda, Lu Yanghao, Yang Kailing, Zhuang Shangyan, Wang Huzhen, (Executive Directors) Shen Donglu, Dong Zuobin, Zhuang Shangyan, Sheng Xinfu, Hu Xingzhi, Zheng Shixu, Lu Yanghao, Yang Kailing, Le Sibing, Jin Songcen, He Zhenya, (Secretary-General) Wei Juxian. The list of members of the Research Committee, Publication Committee, and Investigation Committee is omitted.

Soliciting Investigation

In order to expand the investigation of antiquities, the association specially organized an Investigation Committee, invited the directors of the education bureaus of various counties to serve as ex officio members, and invited history and Chinese teachers from primary and secondary schools in various counties to serve as investigators. The solicitation letter is recorded as follows: "Respected Sir, this association was established to study the ancient culture of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and is named the Wu Yue History and Geography Research Association. Ancient stone tools used by humans before the use of bronze and iron have been discovered in Nanjing in Jiangsu, and Hangzhou, Shaoxing, Yuhang, Huzhou, and other places in Zhejiang. Pottery contemporary with stone tools has also been discovered in Yancheng in Changzhou, Jiangsu, Wucheng and Yuecheng near Shihu Lake in Suzhou, the coast of Jijiadun in Jinshan, and Zhapu in Pinghu, Zhejiang, Ganpu in Haiyan, and Shaoxing. These pottery wares all have geometric patterns printed on them with cloth. This discovery is of great significance to the ancient culture of Wu Yue. People generally believe that Jiangsu and Zhejiang were still barbaric areas in the Spring and Autumn Period. Since the discovery of these stone tools and pottery, it has been proven that Jiangsu and Zhejiang had a very high culture five or six thousand years ago. We now believe that there are many such stone tools and pottery wares in various parts of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Therefore, this association has resolved to establish an Investigation Committee, inviting the directors of the education bureaus of various counties to serve as ex officio members, and inviting history and Chinese teachers from primary and secondary schools in various counties to serve as investigators. In your spare time, after meals, and while walking by rivers, ponds, and small hills, please carefully inspect whether there are stone tools and pottery of the type printed on the back scattered on the ground. If you encounter any, whether complete or broken, pick them up and send a letter detailing the circumstances of the discovery, the shape of the stone tools, and the patterns of the pottery, so that this association can send personnel to investigate. If it is considered necessary to excavate, this association will submit a request to the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee for handling. Discoverers will receive considerable rewards. For this reason, we specially invite you to serve as an investigator and enclose samples of stone tools and pottery with this letter. Please investigate carefully. Sincerely, Correspondence Address: Wei Juxian, Central Bank, No. 15 Bund, Shanghai."

Various Industries Hope That the Money Industry Will Restore the Credit Lending System; Various Firms Believe That It Must Depend on the Creditworthiness of the Other Party 110

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, the Shanghai Money Industry Association has a total of 47 member Huihua money shops, including Fuyuan, which have always regarded credit lending as their main business. Since it has been affected by the decline of the entire market, the number of factories, businesses, and companies that have closed down and gone bankrupt has increased, resulting in the credit system being on the verge of bankruptcy. Money shops have suffered greatly from credit lending. In view of this, the managers of various money shops have had to be particularly cautious about credit lending. Anyone who wants to establish a current account with a money shop and overdraft must have a reliable guarantor, and a overdraft limit will be set to reduce risk. Now, factories, companies, and businesses feel that the turnover of funds is quite difficult after the money shops have tightened credit lending, and they all hope that the money industry will restore the previous credit lending system. However, various money shops accept the principle of restoring the credit lending system, but believe that during this period, it must depend on the creditworthiness of the requesting factories, companies, and businesses.

Subsequently, Tong Hangbai, a standing committee member of the Municipal Party Department, Cheng Haifeng, director of the China Labor Bureau, Lu Jingshi, a member of the Municipal Party Department, and Wang Xianqing, director of the Mediation Section of the Third Division of the Social Bureau, delivered speeches in succession. (Speeches omitted.)

Zhu's Report

Amid enthusiastic applause, Zhu Xuefan stood up and reported on his experiences attending the National Labor Congress and inspecting the labor situation in various countries, briefly stating, "After I arrived in Rome, Italy, by ship, I was concerned about the labor situation in that country. Before Italy entered Rome, the political, diplomatic, and domestic problems were similar to China's situation and situation. After entering Rome, the political situation gradually became on track, with a comprehensive plan for the country and the people. The people's national concept is very strong. When the national affairs were first settled, labor-capital disputes occurred along with it, which was similar to the situation in our country after the Revolutionary Army established its capital in Nanjing in the 16th and 17th years of the Republic of China. The Italian people's leader, Mussolini, at this time, felt deeply about the national conditions and promulgated the Labor Charter, which contained 72 articles, stipulating that factories must not suspend operations without reason, and workers are not allowed to strike. In terms of organization, workers have the National Confederation of Trade Unions, and factories have the General Federation of Industrial Associations. In between, there is the establishment of the Industry Cooperation Department. Working hours, wage levels, etc., have labor-capital contracts signed. When labor-capital disputes occur, they are mediated by the general associations representing both workers and employers. If the two sides cannot resolve the dispute, it is submitted to the Labor Court for adjudication, which is carried out in a prompt manner. Once a ruling is made, both parties must absolutely obey. Any party that violates the ruling will be punished with fines and imprisonment. Since Mussolini took office and promulgated the Labor Charter, the increase in production, the reduction in unemployment, and the stability between labor and capital must be attributed to Mussolini alone. Secondly, the labor situation in Germany is somewhat similar to that in Italy. In 1933, when Hitler came to power in Germany, the labor policy was laissez-faire. The labor organization was complex and took the same position as the Second International. Since Hitler came to power, he was determined to plan and reorganize the domestic labor organization into the Labor Corps. Hitler himself regarded himself as a protector, with advisors under the protector, factory owners as leaders, and workers as followers. He advocated that factory owners must wholeheartedly care for workers, and workers should enthusiastically reward factory owners. Labor and capital jointly set up a collaborative association. Under the collaborative association, there is a trust committee, which is equal to a trade union organization, and is responsible for labor welfare undertakings, investigating factory treatment of workers, and the production situation of workers. Both parties rely on the report of the trust committee. In addition to the trust committee, a supervisory committee is also established to be responsible for supervising all actions of the trust committee. In addition, there is a nominal court. If labor-capital disputes cannot be resolved, they are submitted to the court for disposal. Therefore, Germany's industrial development has surpassed that of European and American countries. Regarding workers' welfare undertakings, the promotion of sports, and proper entertainment, such as travel and swimming, the facilities are very thorough. Special attention is paid to female workers' childbirth. Insurance for death, accidents, and childbirth is exceptionally developed. The people of Italy and Germany love the country, obey the leader, and the executive personnel are impartial and serve the people. This is the spirit of nation-building that our country is worth emulating. In addition, Zhu also reported that there are an estimated one million overseas Chinese workers. Because the motherland is weak, they are often bullied and their lives are not guaranteed. The tragic situation was described in great detail. However, due to space limitations, more will be reported in the future.

Chamber of Commerce Urges the Ministry of Finance to Lift the Prohibition on Flying Flowers 112

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday, saying, "Respectfully to the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: On the 28th of this month, the Shanghai Flying Flowers Industry Association sent a letter stating that the association's member manufacturers were mistakenly listed in the prohibited category by the Jianghai Customs for the Ministry of Finance's prohibition of waste cotton exports. The matter concerns the business of the association's member manufacturers, has a huge impact on the whole, and the public is panicked. The association has sent representatives to the capital and then to Lu to petition the authorities, explaining the point of misunderstanding and prohibiting them together, and presenting the difference between the nature and purpose of waste cotton and flying flowers. On August 14, the representatives returned to Shanghai and reported that Minister Kong had fortunately agreed in person to order the Customs Service to correct the error and restore the original state. The association believes that the petition has been approved, so it is waiting quietly for a clear order, hoping to resume business as soon as possible. Since the export of flying flowers has been mistakenly banned, the business work of member manufacturers has been suspended in both cases, and more than two decades have passed. Not only is the loss incalculable, but the economy has also become difficult, and the lives of tens of thousands of workers have been unable to maintain. Therefore, there is an urgent need to withdraw the ban. For this reason, we urge your association to submit a telegram to the Ministry of Finance based on the facts, and ask the Ministry of Finance to quickly correct the order to mistakenly ban flying flowers, so that the association's industry can restore the original state as soon as possible. The urgency is beyond description. The association has learned that this matter was previously submitted to your department in a telegram on the 5th of this month, asking to handle the ban on exports of flying flowers and waste cotton separately. Subsequently, the association elected representatives to submit a face-to-face report to your department, and cited the fact that Japan does not prohibit the export of flying flowers, and only imports waste cotton as evidence, which is particularly detailed and clear. It is for reference in handling this matter. Subsequently, your department sent a telegram, stating that it had been transferred to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for review and reply, and that it would wait for the government's decision. However, the Yuanri telegram instruction received by the association after submitting this case to the Military Affairs Commission stated that the letter had been forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for review and handling. It is known that although the motive for discussing the ban is related to military affairs, the Military Affairs Commission still allows your department to directly preside over the review and handling of the separate handling of flying flowers and waste cotton, and there is no claim. This is the main point of this case. After reviewing the situation, it should not take a long time due to repeated consultations. At this time, the Customs announced the prohibition of flying flower exports on August 4, and it has been more than 24 days now. Merchants cannot export goods that have already been transacted, and dare not continue to place orders for those that have not been transacted, resulting in huge losses. I hope that your department will review and verify, and quickly handle the matter separately, and send a telegram to the customs to lift the ban, which is for the public good. Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce respectfully bows."

Ministry of Finance: Improving China's Banking Industry; Establishing a Central Reserve Bank to Fulfill Its Mission; Strengthening Commercial Banks to Invigorate Market Finance 113

New News Agency reports: Since the government implemented currency system policies and thoroughly reformed China's finance, it has become stable. The financial authorities are now striving to improve the banking industry, the hub of finance, to systematize it and fully leverage the functions of banks. The details are recorded as follows:

Central Reserve Bank

The central bank is the bank of banks, and the central hub of national finance. Since the establishment of the Central Bank of China, it has achieved considerable results in assisting banks and adjusting finance. For example, in the past two years, the Central Bank, together with the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, has provided substantial loans to directly assist fellow banks and indirectly regulate the market, with significant results. Recently, the Board of Directors resolved to increase its capital stock and reorganize into a Central Reserve Bank to promote bill discounting and open market policies, develop the functions of the central bank, and fulfill its mission as the bank of banks. The reorganization plan is actively underway. Once realized, bank credit will be fully utilized, and agriculture, industry, and commerce are expected to develop rapidly, which will greatly benefit the recovery and progress of the national economy.

Developing Specialized Banks

The specialized banks of China, as stipulated by the financial authorities, are of three types: (1) the Bank of China, a bank for developing international remittance; (2) the Bank of Communications, a bank for developing domestic industries; and (3) the Farmers Bank of China, a bank for developing national agriculture. These three banks each have special operations to complete national economic construction. For example, the Bank of China already has branches in London and Osaka and has recently added branches in New York and Singapore to promote the development of Sino-foreign remittance business. As for the Bank of Communications' efforts to invest in industry and the Farmers Bank of China's widespread implementation of rural lending, both are proceeding step by step according to the original plan. In addition, the Bank of Communications increased government shares, and the Farmers Bank of China changed its name and reorganized, and was specially authorized to issue banknotes with the same legal tender status as the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications. The strength of the three banks is even more robust, and their mutual support in developing China's agricultural and industrial sectors is of great significance.

Strengthening Commercial Banks

Commercial banks are the most common and important banks in the country, and they are closely related to the prosperity and decline of commerce. However, among China's commercial banks, there are still few that are large in scale and have strong capital. In cities, there are more small-scale banks. The disadvantage of this phenomenon is that the strength of each bank is dispersed, business is difficult to develop, and competition among peers increases. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance, in view of this, requires commercial banks to increase capital, strengthen their strength, and concentrate funds to make the bank organization sound, assist commercial development, and invigorate market finance. For example, the recent merger of the Jiangzhe Bank and the China Remittance Bank, the planning of the Four Bright Bank to increase capital, and the adjustment of the business of the Silk Industry Bank have all been implemented step by step to strengthen the internal organization.

Promoting Savings Banks

The business of savings banks in China is limited by investment opportunities, which are narrow and have failed to develop fully. Therefore, there are few purely savings banks in the country that do not engage in other businesses. To promote savings banks, in addition to the Bank of China adding a savings department, the Central Bank has allocated funds to establish the Central Savings Association to encourage public savings habits and concentrate scattered social capital. At the same time, it is striving to develop transportation, public utilities, and open up new avenues for long-term investment. Therefore, this measure not only utilizes surplus funds and develops enterprises but can also create a thrifty atmosphere for society.

Implementing Banking Laws and Regulations

China's banking laws and regulations have been promulgated, and all banks should earnestly abide by them. Now, China's banking system has taken shape. All banking laws and regulations, such as the Central Bank Law, the Banking Law, the Savings Bank Law, the Trust Law, and the Special Bank Regulations, are said to have been decided to be revised in detail and will soon be implemented to protect the rights of depositors. In the future, when commercial banks apply for registration, the total amount of opening capital and the qualifications of the promoters and managers must be strictly examined before approval can be granted. If, after the bank opens, its business scope, operating methods, and business conditions must be subject to official inspection at any time and reported to the Ministry of Finance in a timely and truthful manner to protect the public interest.

Workers from Various Departments of the Anglo-American Third Factory to Petition Today 116

The Ta Kung Pao reports that since the workers of the Anglo-American Tobacco Factory Third Factory (renamed Yizhong Tobacco Company) on Huade Road, Pudong, have been engaging in a go-slow, all work in various departments has come to a standstill, and preparations are being made to recruit new workers. All the workers have submitted eight conditions to petition the party and government organs. However, the factory's attitude is to deal with it resolutely. The details are recorded as follows:

Recruiting New Workers

The factory's entire workforce of male and female workers, in opposition to the harsh treatment of workers by the Chinese manager Wei Ziqian and the dismissal of female workers, has been engaging in a go-slow for two weeks. Since the occurrence of the worker go-slow, work in various departments has completely stopped. In order to maintain operations, it has been decided to recruit new workers to enter the factory to work. However, after the workers received this news, they have formed a team to conduct strict inquiries and monitor the entry of new workers into the factory.

Petition This Morning

The factory notified the striking workers to settle their due wages yesterday, but all the workers, fearing that the factory would take the opportunity to monitor their actions, did not go to the factory to collect them. Yesterday was a weekly holiday. All the workers have decided to go to the Municipal Party Department, the Social Bureau, the General Labor Union, and other organs this morning to petition. At the same time, they will submit the eight conditions agreed upon to the English supervisor Herbert for direct negotiation.

Factory Attitude

The Ta Kung Pao reporter recently inquired with the factory about how to resolve the current turmoil. According to the person in charge, after all the workers engaged in a go-slow, the highest responsible person in the factory had expressed acceptance of the workers' demands, and it could have been resolved earlier. However, the workers insisted that personnel issues be a prerequisite, which is actually interfering with the factory's administration. Now, the factory still hopes that the workers will resume work as soon as possible. As for any demands, it should be discussed at length. If the workers are obsessed, the factory will take resolute measures to maintain operations.

The request is noted and should be approved. In addition to ordering the Shanghai Commissioner Ma Liang for Registering Opium Smokers and Reporting Drug Trafficking to be informed, you are to instruct the Public Security Bureau to register all opium smokers in the city within the deadline, without leaving out any. In accordance with Article 7 of the Measures for Registering Opium Smokers and the instructions of Instruction No. 1019, prepare a statistical summary table of the number of registered opium smokers in the city, together with the city government's affidavit, and submit it to the Commissioner for verification. In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureau to comply, the following announcement is made known to all." This announcement was issued in August of the 25th year of the Republic of China by Mayor Wu Tiecheng and Commissioner Ma Liang.

New News Agency reports that since the Municipal Public Security Bureau received the order to start the total citizen report on opium smokers in this city on May 10, the original deadline was this month, the 10th. After being approved by the Opium Suppression Supervisory Department to postpone it for one month, it was set for September 10th. The reporting of opium smokers will end at the same time as the Opium Suppression Commissioner's Office in this city. The report that the reporting of opium smokers will end on the 31st is slightly inconsistent with the facts. In recent days, the Public Security Bureau has specially ordered its subordinates to intensify the investigation and crackdown work, and Section Chief Dai has gone to each branch to instruct the special police officers in charge of investigation and crackdown to urge them to intensify their work. As of yesterday, statistics show that more than 19,000 people have renewed their licenses in the second phase, more than 21,000 people have registered, and more than 13,000 people have quit opium addiction. More than 100 opium cases are solved every day. There are still many opium smokers quitting in various hospitals. In order to fundamentally eliminate opium smokers, the bureau will handle affidavits of residence after the total reporting deadline.

Gu Zhuxuan Cannot Bear Life in Prison and Seeks Legal Relief; Hopes to Offset Prison Time with Days of Detention; Has Hired Lawyer to Petition Court for Release 121

Gu Zhuxuan, the former owner of the Tianchan Stage, was arrested by the French Concession Police and sent to the Second Special Court for trial in connection with the assassination of Tang Jiapeng. He was sentenced to imprisonment. During the appeal period, he was detained outside the prison for illness and bribed the guards to smoke opium. The prisoners reported him, and the French Police Affairs Department filed a public prosecution. The Second Special Court sentenced him to eight months in prison. Gu refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the High Third Branch Court. As a result, on June 26, the murder case was completely revoked, and the original sentence was declared not guilty. The opium case was still sentenced to eight months in prison, with deprivation of civil rights for one year and abstinence for two months. After the final judgment was made on July 15 and sent to the Second Special Prison for execution, Gu filed a petition with the High Third Branch Court, requesting exemption from abstinence and exemption from the execution of the unexpired prison term. The High Third Branch Court consulted the Institute of Forensic Medicine to send a forensic doctor to assess Gu's opium addiction and confirmed that he had quit. The High Third Branch Court has ruled that Gu Zhuxuan's abstinence punishment is exempt from execution, and the other requests were rejected (i.e., the exemption from the sentence was not allowed). Therefore, after receiving this ruling in prison, calculating the prison term, it will expire on January 12 next year, which is still half a year away. Feeling that life in prison is too bitter, he has recently hired a lawyer to seek other legal relief and has filed a petition with the High Third Branch Court on Gu's behalf, requesting that all the days Gu has been detained since his arrest be offset against the prison term. Gu was arrested by the French Concession Police on September 10 of last year and transferred to the Second Special Court for detention in connection with the Tang Jiapeng assassination case. To date, it has been eleven months and twenty-one days. If all the days of detention are offset against the eight-month prison term for the opium case, he has been detained for three months and twenty-one days more and should be released. It is said that whether the High Third Branch Court will approve this request is still under study by the presiding judge of the High Court, as there is no precedent for this type of request, and there are no provisions in the law to rely on.

Flour Exchange Held Shareholders Meeting Yesterday 126

The Shanghai Flour Exchange held its 17th Second Shareholders Meeting at 2:00 pm yesterday. More than 300 people attended, holding 12,300 shares. Chairman Wang Yiting first reported that the capital stock had been increased by 250,000 yuan at the shareholders' extraordinary meeting on July 28, and that every three old shares could purchase one new share, which had already been fully subscribed, as well as the general business situation for the first half of this year. Then, the following were discussed: (1) Due to the increase in capital stock, two new directors will be added, making a total of eleven, and one supervisor will be added, making a total of three. The resolution was passed. (2) Article 2 of the company's articles of association will be changed to "The total capital stock of the company is 1 million yuan, divided into 20,000 shares, each share is 50 yuan in national currency, and it will be collected in one lump sum." Article 21 will be changed to "The company will have eleven directors and three supervisors, who will be elected by the shareholders' meeting." Article 32 will be changed to "Shareholders of the company who have 50 or more shares are qualified to be elected as directors, and those who have 20 or more shares are qualified to be elected as supervisors." The resolution was passed. (3) One standing director will be added. The resolution was passed. (4) Article 18 of the company's articles of association will be amended. The resolution was amended to "When the shareholders' meeting is held, the board of directors will be the chairman, and the chairman of the board will be the chairman. If the chairman of the board is absent, one person will be publicly elected from the directors present to act on his behalf." The resolution was passed.

This Year's Cotton Production Increases Sharply; Export to Japan is the Only Way Out 128

New News Agency reports that due to favorable weather and abundant agricultural production this year, the cotton harvest has also doubled compared to previous years. The estimated output is about 10 million dan. New cotton has been coming on the market in various places, and the cotton market has gradually become active. The details are recorded as follows:

Coming on the Market One After Another: According to the Cotton Industry Control Association, due to weather conditions, the time for new cotton to come on the market in various places varies by two or three weeks. The first to arrive in Shanghai was the Yuyao cotton from Zhejiang Province, two batches of which have already been transported. Cotton from Tongzhou, Haizhou, Taicang, and other places in Jiangsu Province has also arrived in Shanghai for sale. New cotton from Shaanxi and Henan provinces will have to come on the market one or two weeks later because the climate there is different from that of Jiangsu and Zhejiang.

Only Way Out: The harvest in cotton-producing areas this year is more abundant than in previous years. According to cotton production estimates, the cotton fields in the main cotton-producing areas are more than 50 million mu, producing more than 16 million dan of lint cotton, which is the highest cotton production figure in the past 20 years. However, the estimated national cotton consumption is only about 10 million dan, and there is still a large surplus. The only way out is to rely on low prices to export to Japan.

Price Equilibrium: As new cotton comes on the market, various yarn mills have been buying it one after another, preparing to increase production to meet the needs of the autumn and winter market. The cotton market situation has gradually become active. Due to the abundant cotton harvest this year, coupled with the weak quotations for foreign cotton, the prices are extremely balanced. The opening price of high-grade new cotton is only between 42 and 43 yuan, and the price of September-October futures cotton is also within 40 yuan.
